# Deferred Inventory â€” Standing Index

**Purpose:** canonical register of every deferred epic, deferred story, and named-but-not-filed follow-on across the project. Single source of truth consulted at:

1. **Every Epic retrospective** â€” per [CLAUDE.md Â§Pipeline lockstep regime](../../CLAUDE.md) and Â§Deferred inventory governance, the retrospective MUST review this inventory against the closing Epic's new substrate / evidence / learnings; flag now-ready-to-reactivate entries to the next sprint-planning round.
2. **Every session hot-start** â€” `next-session-start-here.md` surfaces the inventory counts so the operator sees "don't overlook" context every session open.
3. **Story authoring** â€” when a new story spec names a follow-on (e.g., "15-1-lite-irene is a fast-follow after this story"), the author adds the follow-on to Â§Named-But-Not-Filed Follow-Ons below.

**Maintenance:** update at (a) each Epic retrospective close, (b) each story closure that names a new follow-on, (c) any session-wrapup where the operator flags a new deferred item, (d) each forward-port pass on the hybrid migration branch (see Â§Forward-Port Deferred below). ### Gamma Styleguide Library Leg-A follow-ons (2026-07-01; from the Leg-A dual-gate party CLOSE — Murat/Dan/Vera CLOSE-WITH-CONDITIONS)
Parent: `gamma-styleguide-leg-a-library-spine.md` (arc branch `dev/gamma-styleguide-library-2026-07-01`). Leg-A CLOSED; these are the conditions + review residuals.
- ~~🔴 **`styleguide-retire-default-variant-pair`** — RIPE NOW~~ **✅ CLOSED 2026-07-01** (single-gate structural CLOSE, Murat 6/6 bars). `_normalized_gamma_settings` now projects only payload-present variants (`return [by_variant[v] for v in present_ids]`) — a single styleguide binding paid-dispatches EXACTLY ONE deck (AC#8 live-proven: 1 real `generate_deck` call, variant A only, zero fixture-B). Full BMAD spine: GREEN-LIGHT 6/6 (party record `retire-default-variant-pair-greenlight-party-record-2026-07-01.md`) → dev RED-first → 3-lane review (0 MUST-FIX + R1–R4 fail-loud remediation) → AC#8 live proof → CLOSE. Story `styleguide-retire-default-variant-pair.md` (done). Spawned the successor below.
- 🟡 **`styleguide-retire-default-variant-pair-fail-loud-flip`** (filed 2026-07-01 at CLOSE, per Gary/Dan green-light AMEND) — a present-but-styleguide-less variant currently **retains** the `DEFAULT_VARIANT_PAIR` base seed + emits a WARN (honesty-logged; observability only, no output change). Once **`styleguide-cd-envelope-authoring-ceremony`** lands and the library is fully authoritative, **flip the WARN-seed path to FAIL-LOUD** ("a present variant without a bound styleguide is a governance error"). Absorbs Gary's strip-to-neutral-seed proposal (strip-now was rejected as an out-of-scope output-behavior change to the proven concierge A/B default path). **Reactivation trigger:** `cd-envelope-authoring-ceremony` open. Direction-stable (library-or-nothing is the end-state). *Direction may flip if substrate evolves.*
- 🔴 **`styleguide-cd-envelope-authoring-ceremony`** — (Dan CLOSE, AC#6 reframe): the runtime author-and-persist ceremony (CD proposes a versioned `cd_styleguide_library` block through Marcus's envelope; Marcus/operator persists; validator gates the write) is **NOT exercised in Leg A** — the seeds were hand-authored from the draft + passed the write-gate. AC#6 was reframed at CLOSE to Leg-A's actual claim (CD-owned SSOT + validator write-gate + verified read-only resolver). **Reactivation:** the author-and-persist leg (CD write authority through the envelope). Tracks AC#6's original intent so it can't drift out of view.
- 🟡 **`styleguide-inputtext-source-detail-regression-pin`** — (Vera CLOSE): the PROTECTED-INVARIANT charter ([[feedback_source_detail_to_gamma_conveyance_protected]]) names per-slide `inputText`/image prompts, but AC#8 pins only `additional_instructions` + `keywords`. Architecturally safe TODAY (`_input_text` is independent of the styleguide resolver — no seam), so no live degradation. **Cleanup:** add a lightweight pin asserting per-slide `inputText` survives styleguide resolution byte-unchanged, BEFORE any future refactor folds styleguide-derived context into inputText composition. Direction-stable (additive guard; never relaxes fidelity).
- 🟡 **`styleguide-validator-live-existence-hardening`** — the validator `--check-existence` path (OFF by default): fixed limit `100→50` at CLOSE (real Gamma caps at 50), but still (a) does NOT verify Studio **template** existence (only api themes), and (b) does not paginate beyond the first 50 themes. Harden both before relying on it as a live pre-render gate. (Studio template `g_nv5q4da69qiiu8q` was confirmed live in the AC#5 render, but not by the validator.)
- 🟡 **`styleguide-16x9-publication-boundary-safety`** — (committed in the Leg-A spec): the Descript anti-crop OUTCOME the removed 16:9 force provided must be relocated to a **publication-time policy** (or an operator/style choice) so future Descript-bound production runs don't crop. Phase-2 runs stop at Storyboard B (pre-Descript), so no in-arc regression; relocate before any Descript-bound production run under the library.
- 🟢 **`styleguide-duplicate-id-detection`** — (Edge#7): PyYAML silently last-wins on duplicate `style_guides:` ids; neither loader nor validator detects it. Add a custom-loader / pre-scan duplicate-key check so a CD copy-paste can't silently shadow a record.
- 🟢 **`styleguide-level-additional-instructions-inert`** — (Edge#10): a styleguide record's own `prompt_configuration.additional_instructions` is never consumed (Classic reads payload-level only; Studio uses the lock wrapper) — dead config that looks live. Either wire styleguide-level instructions or drop the field from the seed schema.
- 🟢 **`gamma-title-matcher-punctuation-robustness`** — **CONCIERGE BACKLOG (not the styleguide seam):** the bijective export title-matcher fails `gamma.export.brief-unmatched` when a source slide title contains an apostrophe (Gamma slugifies "The Intrapreneur's Maze" → "The-Intrapreneurs-Maze"). Live-hit in the AC#5 first run (worked around by cleaning the TITLE, bodies unchanged). Normalize punctuation/apostrophes in the containment match so legitimately-punctuated source titles bind.
- 🟢 **`styleguide-source-detail-spectrum-same-format-ab`** — **Phase-2 confirmation** (Vera): run a SAME-FORMAT (Classic-vs-Classic) A/B across the LOW/MED/HIGH detail corpus to isolate the operator's source-detail-modulation-of-style hypothesis — the Leg-A Classic-vs-Studio *format* gulf dominated the aspect/size metric, so the hypothesis is proven-non-vacuous but not yet isolated. Operator-eye LOOK verdict.

### Gamma instructions-channel cleanup follow-ons (2026-07-01; from the `gamma-instructions-channel-cleanup` dual-gate CLOSE — operator-surfaced from live runs)
Parent: `gamma-instructions-channel-cleanup.md` (done). Operator principle: `additionalInstructions` is a legitimate/primary style channel, but must never be merely-redundant with, nor contradict, a structured param. The cleanup removed the redundant settings-dump + `image_style=None` bug + vestigial `template=`, de-tokenized keywords to prose guidance. These two extend the frame:
- 🟡 **`gamma-keywords-to-imageoptions-style-channel`** (Gary green-light AMEND) — route style-medium keywords (vector/minimalist/flat-color/linework class) to the STRUCTURED `imageOptions.style` free-text descriptor (a STRONGER Gamma image signal than prose), with source-wins precedence over styleguide-base keywords; genuinely-subject keywords → the per-slide image prompt; prose = last resort only. Render-affecting → needs its own live A/B. Deferred from the cleanup because (a) the operator affirmed prose-as-style is fine and (b) it exceeds a redundancy-removal's scope. *Direction may flip if substrate evolves.*
- 🟡 **`gamma-prose-vs-param-noncontradiction-validator`** — extend the Leg-A `scripts/utilities/validate_gamma_style_guides.py` coherence check to flag a styleguide whose prose `additional_instructions` CONTRADICTS its structured settings (e.g. prose implies photographic while `stylePreset=illustration`). Enforces the operator's NON-CONTRADICTION half of the contract at author-time (the cleanup enforced non-redundancy at emit-time; this closes the other half). Pairs with Leg-B dependency enforcement.
- 🟢 **`gamma-single-slide-deck-title-matcher-flake`** (incidental, observed 2026-07-01) — the bijective export title-matcher (`gamma.export.brief-unmatched`) also fails on SINGLE-slide decks (Gamma adds a cover / rephrases the lone card title), distinct from the apostrophe case in `gamma-title-matcher-punctuation-robustness`. Live-hit twice on single-slide AC#8 attempts (worked around by the known-good 3-slide corpus). Low priority; a live proof should use ≥2 slides or clean single-card titles.

### Leg-B1 dependency-rules follow-ons (2026-07-01; from the `leg-b1-documented-dependency-rules` dual-gate CLOSE — Murat structural + Gary/Dan content CLOSE-WITH-CONDITIONS)
Parent: `leg-b1-documented-dependency-rules.md` (done). B1 landed the warnings channel + Rule 2 (ERROR `gamma.dep.image-model-source`) + Rule 3 (WARN `gamma.dep.preset-style-subordinated`); rules 5/7 + from-template⊕theme_id + rule 6 dropped/deduped honestly. These follow-ons carry the deferred scope (Dan C1 = these must be in the SSOT per governance §3, not the spec alone):
- 🟡 **`gamma-runtime-request-dependency-rules`** (Dan C1 MUST) — the dropped rules 5 (`numCards` only honored when card-count is model-driven; an explicit `card_split` break-set makes numCards moot) + 7 (single `export_as` per generation) guard the **runtime Gamma request assembly**, NOT the styleguide YAML (`num_cards`=`len(slides)` at dispatch; `card_split` hardcoded `inputTextBreaks`; `export_as` a scalar `png`). Validate them where the request is built (`generate_gamma_variants`), not the CD write-gate. **Also confirm** the seed YAML `page_settings.export.export_as: png` is inert/documentary (a CD editing it must not falsely believe it changes output) — if live, either wire it or drop it from the seed schema (Gary condition 3).
- 🟡 **`gamma-styleguide-art-direction-no-op-under-imageless-source`** (Gary Bar 6 — same failure class as Rule 2) — when `image_source ∈ {noImages, placeholder, themeAccent}`, the art-direction fields (`style_preset`/`keywords`/`custom_style`) are ALSO silently discarded — a CD could author a full illustration/keyword stack that never renders. Statically decidable → an ERROR rule of the same shape as Rule 2. Additive strengthening (no seed trips it). Lands naturally with B2 or as a B1-sibling. (Lower-confidence sub-item, investigate-only: `text_mode=preserve` may subordinate `amount` — blueprint seed has preserve+brief.)
- 🟢 **`gamma-styleguide-text-mode-preserve-requires-text`** (Dan C1 MUST — file the named follow-on) — WARN when `text_mode=preserve` with empty/thin authored card text (`preserve`/`condense`/`generate` on empty `inputText` → empty cards). Deferred from B1 as lower-priority.
- 🟢 **`gamma-surface-violation-message-clarity`** (Dan C2 SHOULD, optional) — when `theme` is among the studio surface-violation keys, ENRICH (REPLACE, never double-fire) the generic `gamma.styleguide.surface-violation` message to name the specific conflict ("the studio template is already the theme authority — drop theme.id"). The generic message (which already names `'theme'`) is sufficient to ship; this is polish. Lives in Gary's shared `expand_record`/`styleguide_library.py` (also feeds dispatch) → own small item.

Auditor verdict (acceptable slice cut): the byte-exact TAG-ONLY invariant (`strip_tags(provider)==canonical`) is the primary firewall and IS enforced; the two populated roles (warm_callback STRUCTURAL, contrast_emphasis TONAL) introduce no NEW Irene-authored clinical wording, so no authorship gate is needed yet. **Reactivation trigger:** the FIRST rhetorical role that introduces NEW Irene-authored spoken/clinical wording (a STRUCTURAL role whose callback sentence is generatively authored, not pure-connective). **HARD GATE — DEV-AGENT AUTHORITY CANNOT BYPASS (D3, Vera): that first role does NOT ship until ALL THREE joint preconditions hold (conjunction, not menu of options):** **(a)** `audit_rhetorical_source_containment` is WIRED into the irene/enrique flow (an actual runtime caller that gates generative authorship), **AND** **(b)** the negation/comparator detector is UPGRADED from bag-of-words to span/dependency-aware — the "not increased" vs "increased" flipped-negation false-negative MUST be fixed; bag-of-words must NEVER be the live guard on generative clinical text, **AND** **(c)** a REAL clinical lexicon is supplied (not the default-off `clinical_terms` stub). Any one of (a)/(b)/(c) missing ⇒ the role is BLOCKED from shipping; this is a party-gated reactivation, not a dev-agent cleanup. Direction-stable (additive gate; never relaxes the figure-citation gate).

### concierge-leg1a follow-ons (2026-06-30; from the Leg-1a 3-layer code-review)
- 🟡 **`directed-voice-override-cannot-suppress-rhetorical-role`** — Parent: `concierge-leg1a-rhetorical-role-emission.md` (Edge Case Hunter Finding #2). Now that `rhetorical_role` is live on the role-derived seed, an operator `voice_direction_overrides` entry for a synthesis segment can REPLACE the role with another populated role but **cannot SUPPRESS it to `None`** — `voice_direction_annotation._overlay` (`:117-127`) skips `None` values, so an override of `{rhetorical_role: None}` is ignored and `contrast_emphasis` survives (and on a v3 run the `[slow]` tag still rides). This is consistent with the pre-existing None-suppression limitation for tone fields, and Leg-1a's scope is narrow (synthesis→contrast_emphasis only; no operator workflow yet overrides rhetorical_role per-segment), so it is NOT a Leg-1a blocker (party-ratified at CLOSE 2026-06-30). **Cleanup:** give the override tier a way to clear a role-derived `rhetorical_role` (e.g. a sentinel `"neutral"`/`"none"` rhetorical value the compiler treats as no-tag, or `_overlay` honoring an explicit `None` for an allowlisted suppress-key). **Reactivation trigger:** when an operator needs per-segment suppression of a role-derived directed read, OR when Leg-1b/role-widening makes multiple roles emit (raising the odds an operator wants to veto one). Direction-stable (additive override capability; never relaxes a gate).

The remaining M-2 rows (G1 locked-lesson-plan, G2C authorized-storyboard, G3/G4/G4A voice-selection / pass2-envelope / synthesis) are NOT yet pinned because their run-dir path is not reliably materialised (the CF-A run's `exports/` was empty — storyboard publish stubbed). **Action:** for each, confirm the real on-disk path + digest_algo (CANONICAL_SHA256 for JSON, FILE_CONTENT_SHA256 for YAML/binary) and add the row (the gate writer no-ops harmlessly on any absent file, so each row is a side-effect-free one-line extension), OR absent-seed it. Direction-stable.
- 🟢 **`udac-v1-fail-loud-on-gate-crossed-absent-asset`** — Parent: UDAC v1 code-review F4 (2026-06-28). The v1 dispatch guard keys off RAI `authority_status`, so a consumer requiring an asset whose `produced_by_node` gate HAS crossed but whose file never reached the RAI (gate-crossed-but-asset-not-flushed) fails OPEN rather than loud. **Action:** thread gate-position (`last_gate_crossed`/node index) into the dispatch guard so "required asset whose gate is behind us but is unindexed" RAISES (tagged) instead of silently passing. F3 (ratify on every gate-crossing branch, landed in v1) reduces but does not eliminate the surface. **Trigger:** when UDAC enforcement is promoted from flag-gated to default-on, or before relying on UDAC to catch a dropped-asset regression. Direction caveat: revalidate against the universality map state (a fuller GATE_ASSET_MAP shrinks the residual).
- 🔵 **`lo-ratify-gate-a8-reconfirm`** — Parent: G0-S1 T11 (Acceptance Auditor) → **S3 scope**. `advance_lo(ratified, "ratified", operator)` is a silent idempotent no-op; ratification §2-A8 requires a touched prior-`ratified` LO to get an EXPLICIT operator re-confirm, never a silent re-stamp. A8 targets the S3 ratify-gate HANDLER, not the pure guard. **Action:** S3's gate #2 handler must implement the re-confirm and not lean on `advance_lo` idempotency (already encoded in `g0-s3-irene-refinement-loop.md` AC-S3-4).

- 🟢 **`directed-voice-pause-padding-compositor-wiring`** — Parent: Step-4 code-review (Edge S5). - 🟢 **`directed-voice-enrique-resume-idempotency-double-spend`** — Parent: Step-4 code-review (Edge S2). **PARTIALLY ADDRESSED at Step 4:** `build_assembly_bundle` now has a contained per-segment skip-if-exists guard (`_reusable_receipt`) — a re-run reuses a prior paid mp3 iff its receipt records the SAME resolved settings + voice_id (else re-synthesize), so the validation-error partial-spend half (S1) AND the same-settings re-run half no longer double-bill within Enrique. Pinned by `test_s2_rerun_with_existing_segment_skips_api` + `test_s2_rerun_with_changed_settings_resynthesizes`. **Residual (filed):** the runner only skips a COMPLETED enrique node; a mid-loop API error that leaves the node incomplete still re-enters `build_assembly_bundle` on resume — now mostly cushioned by skip-if-exists, but a runner-level "enrique node is segment-resumable" contract (checkpoint per-segment completion) is the full fix. **Trigger:** UDAC (Step 8.5, threads run-asset state through both walks) or a mid-batch-failure trial. Direction-stable.
- 🟡 **`p5-s2-teaches-after-narration-callbacks`** — Parent: Step-6 (P5-S2) green-light party (Gary/Irene/CD/Murat/Winston, unanimous; Consumer C DEFERRED). Use `PedagogyAnnotation.teaches_after` to let Irene Pass-2 emit connective callback phrases ("now that we've seen X…"). DEFERRED from Step 6 because it is LLM narration-AUTHORING (new text) + grounding-sensitive — it cannot meet the deterministic anti-tautology bar that Consumers A+B meet, and forcing it would require either a tautological test or a flaky live gate on model output. **BINDING constraints when built (IR-C1 + MUR-6 — non-negotiable):** a callback may reference a prior component ONLY if (a) it is strictly-before via `teaches_after` AND (b) that component's `PedagogyAnnotation.teachable is True` (`teaches_after` ALONE is insufficient — it can point at ungrounded/`teachable=False` components; that is the ungrounded-callback trap); the callback introduces NO new numeral/figure/claim; it is generated by a pass through the SAME figure-citation gate as all narration (the gate is the entry PRECONDITION); fail-safe SILENT when no matched prior GROUNDED segment. **Trigger:** a future narration-richness iteration once A+B ship. Direction-stable (grounding non-negotiable).
- 🟠 **`directed-voice-slower-pace-value-underpowered`** — Parent: Step-7 / Step-6-A-live terminal demo (2026-06-28, live finding across 2 real runs, first-run-stands, NOT retried-to-green). The role→voice map resolves `pace=slower` to ElevenLabs `speed=0.94`, which does NOT reliably lengthen a clip vs `neutral` (speed=1.0): two identical-text neutral clips already differ by ~0.42s, and the 0.94 effect is swamped by that per-render nondeterminism floor. Worse, the §F.1 `PEDAGOGICAL_ROLE_TO_VOICE` map only ever emits `slower`/`neutral` (worked_example/synthesis/assessment→slower; definition/motivation/practice→neutral) — **no `pedagogical_role` maps to `faster`**, and `faster` (speed≈1.1) was the ONLY pace pole that audibly separated in the Step-5 acoustic audition. Net: Consumer-A role-driven narration delivery is wired correctly and the role-differentiated settings ARE sent live and recorded in receipts (proven — synthesis/worked_example speed=0.94 vs definition speed=1.00, distinct request IDs), but its AUDIBLE role-differentiation is underpowered with the current frozen table. The CONTRACT + wiring are DONE + live-proven; this is value-tuning for audibility, not a pipeline defect. **Action (tuning, party-reviewed before applying — re-audition with the MUR-4 acoustic judge after):** (1) lower the `slower` speed (e.g. 0.85) for a perceptible slowdown; AND/OR (2) map a role to `faster` (e.g. practice/motivation→faster) so the audible pole actually fires; AND/OR (3) add a prosody/stability dial so role-delivery differs audibly beyond duration. Reuse already-captured Step-7 clips offline before any new ElevenLabs spend. **Trigger:** before relying on AUDIBLE role-paced narration in a shipped lesson. Sibling of `directed-voice-energy-scalar-and-best-effort-labeling` (both are "settings are sent but the listener-perceptible tell is underpowered" — a palette/value-tuning class). Direction-stable. Evidence: `evidence/p5-directed-voice-s7-terminal-descript-20260628T024652Z.md` + `...-s6-live-narration-aligned-20260628T024652Z.md`.
- 🟢 **`directed-voice-energy-scalar-and-best-effort-labeling`** — Parent: Step-5 CLOSE party (Murat/Quinn-R/CD/Enrique, unanimous). MUR-4 PASSED on pace→duration (clean reliable tell); energy→broadband-RMS FAILED the 3×floor bar (Δ0.0018 < 0.0099) — an honest measurement-PROXY finding, NOT a pipeline defect (the stability/style settings ARE sent per receipts; ElevenLabs spends them on timbre/prosody, not loudness — RMS is the wrong scalar). **Action (follow-on, NOT a same-run retry):** (1) re-measure energy with a perception-aligned scalar — integrated **LUFS / A-weighted loudness** + an **F0-variance / spectral-centroid** expressiveness proxy (Enrique: switch the SCALAR first; reuse the 5 already-captured Step-5 clips offline before any new spend; optionally then widen the energy palette separation); (2) add a **best-effort label** to the Storyboard B voice-direction panel for tone/energy (pace shown as the guaranteed dial). **Trigger:** next directed-voice iteration / before broader expressive product claims. Direction-stable. Evidence: `evidence/p5-directed-voice-s5-live-acoustic-proof-20260627T231354Z.md`.
- 🟠 **`p5-s2-role-seed-robust-source-to-final-slide-linkage`** — Parent: Step-6 (P5-S2) bmad-code-review (EDGE-1, HIGH, production-correctness). The narration role-derived voice seed currently joins the G0 card's SOURCE-corpus slide ordinals ("Slide 1".."Slide 6") to the FINAL deck's `slide_id` ordinals ("slide-01"..) **by ordinal value**. These are TWO DIFFERENT ordinal spaces: Pass-1 clustering splits dense source slides into sub-slides and RENUMBERS the final deck (a 6-source-slide deck becomes `slide-01..slide-11`), `ignore`-partition drops remove slides, and reorders shuffle them — so card-ordinal N ≠ final-ordinal N in general. **Shipped mitigation (conservative fail-open):** the specialist runs a DIVERGENCE GUARD — it applies role seeds ONLY when the source-slide-ordinal SET (threaded from the card) and the final-deck slide-ordinal SET COINCIDE 1:1; on ANY divergence (count mismatch / membership mismatch / clustering renumber) it emits NO seeds (neutral built-in), never a mis-seed. Voice is delivery-only so a fail-open neutral is harmless; a wrong-role seed mis-paces a real learner segment and is not. Consequence: in real Gary-generated decks (where the source's "Slide N" enumeration rarely equals the generated deck's slide set) seeding fails open and the feature is inert — it fires only when the source and final slide enumerations genuinely align (e.g. a preserve-the-source-deck run or a curated slice). **Durable fix (this entry):** replace the ordinal join with a CONTENT-GROUNDED linkage — match by component `source_ref`/content fingerprint ↔ segment provenance, OR thread Pass-1's source-slide→final-slide cluster map (the authoritative split/drop/reorder record) into the projection so role seeds survive clustering. **Trigger:** when role-derived voice is wanted on clustered/real-Gary-deck trials (the current guard makes it a no-op there). Direction-stable (fail-open is the correct interim posture; the durable join only ADDS coverage, never relaxes the guard). Evidence/in-code: `app/marcus/orchestrator/enrichment_consumption.py` (`project_role_derived_voice_by_slide` NOTE) + `app/specialists/irene/graph.py` (`_role_derived_seeds_for_deltas` EDGE-1 guard). **➕ Step-8 CF-A E2E finding (2026-06-28, Murat/Winston condition):** the fragility is WORSE than clustering alone — `slide_ordinal_from_locator` requires the narration component locator to TERMINATE exactly in `Slide N`, but live gpt-5 NON-DETERMINISTICALLY appends `> Narration` (~half of 5 live runs), yielding an unparseable locator → the guard correctly fail-safes to NO seed. So even on a 1:1-aligned deck the voice-seed is non-deterministically inert depending on the model's locator formatting (it DID fire on trial `8a997d43` where the locator was clean: `by_slide={1,3,6}`). The durable content-grounded linkage must also be robust to locator-suffix variance (don't depend on an exact `Slide N` terminal). This gates a single-run all-in-one CF-A demo (where the ungrounded leg AND the voice-seed leg co-occur in one sampling); both legs are each proven on real runner runs today, just not the same sampling.
- 🔵 **`directed-voice-adjacency-anti-jitter-audition`** — Parent: green-light (CD AM-6) + Step-3 CLOSE (CD). Storyboard B reviews each segment's direction in isolation; there is no cross-segment adjacency/jitter flag (e.g. urgent→reflective→urgent whiplash). Rubric §4 frames coherence as an audition-bench concern, not a Storyboard-B gate requirement. **Action:** add a >1-step adjacent-dial-swing flag in the audition lane (Step 5) / a future Storyboard-B coherence pass. Non-blocking; per-segment review is complete + honest without it.

### P5 directed-voice arc — Step-9 NEXT-INCREMENT reactivation (2026-06-28; party Marcus/John/CD/Murat, UNANIMOUS, no impasse)

The P5 directed-voice arc CLOSED (Steps 1–8 + 8.5 UDAC + §10-item-5 ElevenLabs sweep all signed off; loop live-proven enriched-corpus→deck+role-paced-narration→published-Descript-lesson). Step-9 party ruled the NEXT increment is **E — "make the directed voice REAL" (harden-first)**: the headline feature ships at the PLUMBING level but is **inert on real decks** (role-seed fail-opens to neutral under clustering + gpt-5 locator variance) and **inaudible when it fires** (slower=0.94 under a ~0.42s render floor; no role maps to `faster`). SSOT for the full ruling + ready-for-dev shape + success bar: `p5-directed-voice-arc-strawman-2026-06-27.md §S`. Reactivation verdicts:

- **➡️ REACTIVATED as the E bundle (next session, into a `bmad-create-story` chain — routing rec, not a substitute for the greenlight gate):** three already-filed entries graduate together into increment E:
  - `p5-s2-role-seed-robust-source-to-final-slide-linkage` (EDGE-1, HIGH) — **E-leg 1 (the hard gate):** content-grounded role→slide linkage (key on `lo_refs`/`pedagogical_role`/content fingerprint or the Pass-1 cluster map, NOT ordinal position) so seeds FIRE on clustered/real-Gary decks. **Murat precondition:** confirm the join is LLM-free, then a deterministic source→final slide-map fixture is an honest RED-first pin.
  - `directed-voice-slower-pace-value-underpowered` — **E-leg 2:** widen pace range (slower→~0.85 + map a role→`faster`) AS a **coordinated per-role pace+stability(+style) gesture** (CD binding: pace alone is below the JND; stability is the real perceptual lever).
  - `directed-voice-energy-scalar-and-best-effort-labeling` — folds into E-leg 2's expressiveness dial (LUFS/F0 re-audition of the energy tell rides along).
  - **➕ `seed` (from the §10-item-5 sweep) is an INGREDIENT of E, not a competing increment** — graduate `seed` into the directed-TTS contract to collapse the ~0.42s render-nondeterminism floor that eats the pace tell (byte-identical determinism sweep-confirmed live; trivially RED-first hash-pinnable). **E success bar:** voice FIRES (not fail-open) on ≥1 real clustered Gary deck + Step-5 MUR-4 verifier shows a pace delta exceeding the seed-collapsed floor, cross-confirmed on a 2nd deck, AND **ear-proven blind A/B** (operator can't blind-call → not cleared).
- 🟡 **`p5-cross-corpus-beta`** (NEW, Step-9 #2) — run the full closed loop on a DIFFERENT (and/or multiple) real corpus to prove GENERALITY + act as the forcing function for whether the audible tell matters across content. **Trigger:** immediately after E lands (the loop must carry real value before generality is worth proving). Live-integration, not a deterministic unit increment. Direction-stable.
- 🔵 **`p5-text-to-dialogue`** (NEW, Step-9 #3) — graduate the modeled-but-inert `dialogue_turns`/`render_strategy="dialogue"` path to real two-voice synthesis. **HELD one slot behind E** (ideally after C). **Murat precondition to open safely (binding):** freeze a `dialogue_turns` fixture (fixed input text) + pin ONLY the synthesis+grounding leg deterministically (existing MUR-4 acoustic judge + UDAC grounding firewall — every spoken numeral/token present in the frozen turns); the LLM-authoring leg is verified SEPARATELY + operator-gated, NEVER via a deterministic content-equivalence assertion. Without the input-freeze split it inherits the `teaches_after`/narration-callback deferral problem → STAYS deferred. Direction-stable.
- 🔵 **`directed-voice-apply-text-normalization-grounding-review`** (NEW, Step-9; from the sweep's D-split) — `apply_text_normalization` (sweep-ACCEPTED: auto/on/off) MUTATES spoken text (numeral/acronym reads), so it is **grounding-firewall-sensitive** — it can perturb what the VO is allowed to say vs what's on-slide. **Defer-with-flag:** requires its OWN grounding-impact review before adoption; travels with the dialogue/narration-authoring risk class, NOT with `seed`. Do NOT bundle into E casually. `output_format` (also sweep-ACCEPTED) = cosmetic-tier, defer; not worth a story alone.
- 🔵 **`p5-media-placement-gate`** (NEW, Step-9; named-not-scoped) — a gate that decides/places figures/b-roll/motion into BOTH the deck and the narration timeline. Biggest new surface of the Step-9 menu; no spec, no seam, spans two subsystems. **Stays deferred:** needs its own PRD/architecture chain (`bmad-create-prd`) + a verification-shape spike (rule-driven map vs LLM/aesthetic judgment?) before it is even a story. Direction-stable.

### P5-arc P2 (Texas pass-0) follow-ons (2026-06-26; from P2 design + T11 + party CLOSE)
- 🟡 **`p2-pubmed-adapter-v2`** — Parent: P2 Texas pass-0 (`p2-texas-pass0-design-strawman-2026-06-26.md`; party R2 chose A5=scite-only-v1). scite's index has a coverage gap: a valid biomedical DOI NOT in scite's index returns the same `total:0` as a garbage DOI → real citations mark `failed/not_in_index` (honest, never fabricated, but caps recall). Bare PubMed-URL citations (no DOI, e.g. slice `c014` `pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/31589283`) also can't resolve via scite. **Cleanup:** add a `pubmed` `RetrievalAdapter` (wrap the PubMed MCP tool; deterministic query/refine; `identity_key` DOI/PMID; `get_article_metadata`/`convert_article_ids` for bare-id→metadata). **Trigger:** when citation-resolution recall on biomedical corpora matters for a real (non-demo) deliverable. Direction-stable. Live-proven gap evidence: `evidence/p2-live-citation-resolution-2026-06-26.json`.
- 🟢 **`p2-doi-multi-per-excerpt`** — Parent: P2 T11 (Edge-Case). `extract_doi` returns the FIRST DOI only; a second cited paper in one excerpt is silently dropped (DD4 models 1 resolution/component). **Cleanup:** per-DOI resolution rows when an excerpt carries multiple DOIs. Low priority.
- 🔵 **`p2-universal-md-body-marker-collision-guard`** — Parent: P2 T11 (NIT) → **P5 body parser**. The `<<<CLEAN_BODY>>>`/`<<<PROVENANCE_ANNOTATION>>>` demarcation is string-concatenated with no escape if a verbatim excerpt literally contains a sentinel. Add an escape/guard when the P5 body-splitter is built. Course content unlikely to trip it today.
- 🔴 **`p2-condition1-wired-live-run` + `p2-condition3-live-a4`** — Parent: P2 party CLOSE (Murat, BINDING). The one-process live `build_enrichment_result(dispatch_live=True)` must show BOTH `resolved` and `failed` in one live output, AND A4 `ungrounded` must be exercised on LIVE output. Blocked at P2 only by P1 gpt-5 extraction latency (resolver proven non-hanging; OpenAI responsive). **These RIDE THE FINAL-INTEGRATION E2E (which runs build_enrichment_result live anyway). If the final E2E skips them, P2 is RETROACTIVELY NOT-CLOSED.** Not a formality — a real gate. SSOT: `p5-arc-party-record-2026-06-26.md §P2 PARTY CLOSE`.

| **SciteProvider OAuth 2.1 migration + production-class MCP integration** (`5a-2-scite-mcp-oauth-integration`) | M3 ceremony probe 2026-04-27 in operator session; further-substantiated by 2026-04-27 heartbeat + ceremony successful end-to-end runs | **Candidate Slab 6.2 story** (paired with `migration-6-1-production-graph-runner.md` Slab 6 opener). Third A16 (Composition-vs-Component Audit Gap) instance surfaced when M3 ceremony attempted Scite MCP. Existing `skills/bmad-agent-texas/scripts/retrieval/scite_provider.py` is structurally wrong against the real MCP on **four** dimensions: (1) auth — hardwired to HTTP Basic but real MCP requires OAuth 2.1 Bearer per WWW-Authenticate header pointing at `https://api.scite.ai/.well-known/oauth-protected-resource`; (2) **tool count — assumes 3 separate tools (`search`, `paper_metadata`, `citation_contexts`) but real MCP exposes only ONE unified tool: `search_literature`** (verified 2026-04-27 via heartbeat + ceremony); (3) parameter names — assumes `query`/`max_results` but actual schema is `term`/`limit` plus 27 other rich filter params (year, journal, author, paper_type, retraction filters, smart-citation count ranges, etc.); (4) response shape — assumes per-tool result envelopes but actual response is `{total: int, count: int, query: str, limit: int, offset: int, hits: [{doi, title, authors, ...}]}` wrapped in MCP TextContent. Operator-session ceremony bypasses legacy `SciteProvider` via official `mcp` Python SDK's `OAuthClientProvider` — working reference implementation at `scripts/operator/m3_texas_ceremony_scite.py` + heartbeat at `scripts/operator/scite_heartbeat.py`. Live verified 2026-04-27: real scholarly results returned (53.8M-paper corpus; 5 papers per default query; DOI + title + authors per hit). | **Provider migration, ~5-6pt** (revised up from initial ~2-3pt estimate after 2026-04-27 findings doubled the migration scope). Update `skills/bmad-agent-texas/scripts/retrieval/scite_provider.py` to use OAuth 2.1 via `OAuthClientProvider`: (a) replace `auth_style="basic"` MCPServerConfig with OAuth-aware client construction (mirror reference impl in `scripts/operator/m3_texas_ceremony_scite.py`); (b) implement TokenStorage backed by repo-managed cache directory; (c) **collapse 3-tool assumption to 1-tool — replace `_SCITE_TOOL_SEARCH/PAPER/CITATIONS` constants with single `_SCITE_TOOL_LITERATURE = "search_literature"`**; (d) migrate parameter mapping from `RetrievalIntent` to `search_literature` schema (term, limit, offset + rich filters); (e) migrate response normalization from per-tool shape assumptions to actual `{total, count, hits: [{doi, ...}]}` shape; (f) live integration test gated `pytest -m live` exercising the unified tool; (g) deprecate `SCITE_USER_NAME` + `SCITE_PASSWORD` env vars (no longer needed for MCP); (h) ensure cross-validation with Consensus (per existing contract) still works given the unified-tool shape. | **`slab-7-inter-gate-conversational-orchestration`** *(supersedes the narrower `production-runner-texas-directive-composition-seam` framing — first filed and within-session corrected after operator review of legacy v4.2 prompts 01/02/02A/03)* | First tracked trial 2026-04-28 (`trial_id: 475df528-7d75-48a3-be56-82b54a0b7b8b`). Trial reached `paused-at-gate G1 (gate_focus: trial_open)` cleanly; production-runner end-to-end plumbing verified (gate pause, checkpointer, LangSmith trace, decision card, cost report, `production_clone_launch_evidence: true`). However Texas's contribution at nodes 02/03 returned the deterministic fixture bundle at `tests/fixtures/specialists/texas/fixture_bundle/` (10 lines of placeholder content) — NOT the operator's Tejal APC C1-M1 corpus. Real cost was $0.000005. **Critically:** post-trial operator-review of legacy v4.2 prompts 01–03 (full text quoted in 2026-04-28 evening session transcript) revealed that this is NOT a single missing-module gap — it is **systemic loss of inter-gate conversational orchestration** across the migration. The legacy prompt pack v4.2 has detailed per-section conversational prompts (01 Activation + Preflight, 02 Source Authority Map with file-by-file role assignment HIL, 02A Operator Directives with 3-min-min poll, 03 Ingestion where Marcus AUTHORS `directive.yaml` from §2 + §2A) — every one of these prompts encodes operator-Marcus conversation that the migrated runtime currently barrels through autonomously. Without these conversational gates, downstream specialists (Vera, Irene, Gary, Kira, Quinn-R, ElevenLabs, Compositor, etc.) lack their inputs and produce fixture-stub or empty contributions. **The same shape of "surprise" will reappear at every gate transition** (G1→G1A, G1A→G2C, G2C→G3, G3→G4, etc.) until inter-gate conversational orchestration is restored systemically. | **Three layers missing in the migrated runtime:** **(1) Early-gate HIL pause discipline** — manifest declares G0/G0A/G0B as gates, but production runner only pauses at terminal gates (G1/G2C/G3/G4). All early operator-confirmation gates (legacy "Wait for explicit GO" cadence) are skipped. Same shape will affect any in-between gate the runner doesn't honor. **(2) Conversational composition surface** — no Marcus-runtime interface to author `source-authority-map.md`, `operator-directives.md`, or any other conversational artifact at gate-paused state. Decision cards today only carry `verb: approve` binary verdicts; there is no mechanism for operator to enter/edit prose like file-role assignments or directive content. Maya UI is the deferred candidate but undefined in scope. **(3) Inter-gate composition logic** — once §2 + §2A artifacts exist, no code reads them and emits `directive.yaml` for Texas; Marcus-the-persona did this manually in legacy. Single-epic decomposition ratified unanimously (4/4) on the basis that one terminal full-matrix firing has higher statistical power than three smaller epic-close firings. **Round-2 update (Murat AMEND-7b):** Wave-3 per-surface overlap with Wave-2 (10 HIL stories opening as predecessors land) creates joint-distribution aggregation hazard not covered by single-surface canary; when 3 HIL surfaces share a transport, flake events are NOT independent and 0.1% per-cell budget assumed independence. Lightweight; catches aggregation hazard without adding tripwire ceremony. **Round-2 also tightens budget per AMEND-7a:** 7c-added cells use <0.05% (5e-4) budget; pre-7c cells grandfather at 0.1%. | **TEA conditional follow-on, ~0.5pt at activation.** Author wave-canary as a sub-tripwire under TW-7c-6 (conditional 5-run wave-3-boundary parity firing) ONLY IF Slab 7c slab-close 50-run firing observes flake-rate breach (>0.05% on 7c-added cells; >0.1% on pre-7c) OR Pearson r > 0.3 across any HIL-surface flake pair OR any wave introduces >8 net cell-additions.   <br>**(historical detail)** Original 2026-06-25 framing + wiring: **The original "premium account tier" framing was incomplete.** Re-investigation with the operator's premium scite.ai account (jcph@jefferson.edu) showed the real blocker is the **auth MECHANISM**: `https://api.scite.ai/mcp` requires **OAuth 2.0 Bearer** (`www-authenticate: Bearer`, `.well-known/oauth-protected-resource`). Its authorization server advertises ONLY `authorization_code` + `refresh_token` grants (PKCE S256, public client, dynamic registration) — **no password / client-credentials grant**, so a username/password CANNOT be turned into a Bearer header headlessly (the runner's `SciteProvider` was sending HTTP-Basic, which the server ignores → 401). The premium account is real (the claude.ai Scite + Consensus connectors return live cited results with it). **Wiring landed (Claude-direct, RED-first, 28 offline tests + 15-contract lint-imports green, no regression):** `skills/bmad-agent-texas/scripts/retrieval/scite_oauth_token.py` (load + headless refresh), `SciteProvider._client()` now prefers the OAuth Bearer when a token exists (falls back to Basic), `scripts/operator/scite_oauth_login.py` (one-time interactive authorization_code+PKCE loopback sign-in → persists `secrets/scite_oauth_token.json`, gitignored). **TO CLOSE AC-O1 — single operator action:** run `.venv\Scripts\python.exe scripts\operator\scite_oauth_login.py`, sign in to the premium scite.ai account in the browser that opens + approve (~30s; refresh_token reused thereafter — no repeat). Then a live trial with `MARCUS_RESEARCH_DISPATCH_LIVE=1` dispatches Tracy→Texas→live Scite→≥1 cited entry. (Alt path still open: set `CONSENSUS_API_KEY` Bearer in `.env` for the Consensus provider, which uses a static key not OAuth.) First-run-stands, no mock. Capability-overlay keeps classifying the research path as `present-but-unrouted` until a real trial dispatches it.

## Forward-Port Deferred (hybrid-only, migration branch)

**Context:** the hybrid clone's `dev/langchain-langgraph-foundation` branch runs under FR60 forward-port freeze (ACTIVE since 2026-04-22). Wholesale `git merge upstream/master` is off-policy; per-capability forward-port through the [migration-guide Â§8 reconciliation checklist](../../docs/dev-guide/langgraph-migration-guide.md) is the convergence path. **Probe finding (2026-05-19, post-Slice-D revert):** TW-7c-4's scope is **broader than the orchestrator and Round-2 party-mode appreciated**. The tripwire has TWO assertions: line 56 enforces `app_scope == []` (no `app/`-layer Python touches, which is the freeze condition everyone in Round 2 reasoned about); line 65 ALSO enforces `unexpected == []` against the full `touched_python` set — **forbidding ANY working-tree Python file change outside the 5-path `PERMITTED_PYTHON_DIFFS` allowlist**, regardless of directory. Slice D (`git rm tests/migration/test_slab_2c_next_session_start_here_updated.py`) fired the second assertion despite being a pure `tests/` deletion. Implication: **only edits to (a) non-Python files (YAML / JSON / Markdown / TOML / etc.) or (b) the 5 allowlisted Python paths are truly freeze-safe during pre-Trial-3.** This materially narrows the in-session housekeeping surface; most catalogued failures in `broad-regression-baseline-2026-05-07.md` require Python edits and are structurally blocked until post-Trial-3 substrate amendment.

Slice D has been added to the `s6-housekeeping-coverage-manifest-path-pin-probe` evidence bundle as a paired finding: same root-cause class (post-S6 substrate-currency drift), same architectural disposition (revert + capture + post-Trial-3 reactivation), same `bmad-correct-course` pre-drafted motion at `.tmp/slice-a-post-trial-3-correct-course-draft.md` (motion §1 will be expanded at dispatch time to include the Slice D test-file deletion alongside the Slice A path-pin update).

The hot-start launch command prefix `$env:PYTHONIOENCODING="utf-8"` is PowerShell syntax; on CMD it returns "The filename, directory name, or volume label syntax is incorrect" and is silently no-op. ## ~~CRITICAL Trial-3-blocking — §02A composer downstream-consumer schema-drift~~ (filed 2026-05-21T22:30; CLOSED 2026-05-22)

**Status:** **CLOSED 2026-05-22 via Epic 34** (`migration-34-1-section-02a-wrangler-integration-roundtrip-test` through `migration-34-7-translator-deletion-anti-pattern-entries-epic-close`; commit range `bc477ed..1b59487`). Phase B Quinn-synthesis Option 5 ratified the integration-ratchet-first sequence; Story 34-1 installed the Section 02A -> Texas wrangler subprocess ratchet (bc477ed); Stories 34-2 through 34-4 harmonized the wrangler/schema substrate (cabf850 + 08dfc4a + 16e36f7); Story 34-5 pinned translator shrinkage (e59b0f4); Story 34-6 deleted the legacy composer (55a4d25); Story 34-7 deleted the temporary translator scaffold + filed A23/P5 anti-pattern entries + this closure marker (1b59487). Trial-3 attempt-3 is unblocked on fully harmonized substrate with no temporary translator and no legacy directive composer.

~~Second occurrence in the same trial-launch arc of "tested module, untested integration" defect class. The first occurrence (§02A composer not wired into trial CLI) was patched via SCP-2026-05-21-trial3-wiring; the wiring fix REVEALED the second occurrence at the §02A composer → Texas wrangler integration boundary. **Operator-directed halt of Trial-3 attempt-2** at this finding (2026-05-21T22:30): rather than patch the symptom (one schema-drift gap) and risk discovering further gaps one-at-a-time, batch the full systemic fix.~~

**Observed at:** Trial-3 attempt-2 re-launch 2026-05-21T22:00 against `course-content/courses/tejal-apc-c1-m1-p2-trends/`. Run-id `6a3393f8-f369-4a30-b7c1-b50c60c1d1a2`. Operator confirmed `c` at G0. Texas dispatch raised `BundleDispatchError('texas wrangler reported hard error (exit 30); bundle not trusted')` from [app/specialists/texas/_act.py:323](../../app/specialists/texas/_act.py#L323).

**Root cause (verified by reproducing the wrangler subprocess directly):** the §02A composer's `Directive` schema diverges from the Texas wrangler's expected input schema along multiple field/enum boundaries. Three known incompatibilities surfaced so far; more may exist deeper in the wrangler validation, and additional drift is likely at other downstream surfaces (Texas bundle → Irene Pass-1, Irene packet → §04 G1, etc.) that this trial never reached.

| §02A composer emits | Texas wrangler expects | Wrangler enforcement | Severity |
|---|---|---|---|
| `src_id` | `ref_id` | [run_wrangler.py:319-348](../../skills/bmad-agent-texas/scripts/run_wrangler.py#L319-L348) | Hard fail at validation; this is what crashed attempt-2 |
| `role: supporting` | `role: supplementary` | [run_wrangler.py:328-338](../../skills/bmad-agent-texas/scripts/run_wrangler.py#L328-L338) (allowed set: primary / validation / supplementary / visual-primary / visual-supplementary) | Would hard-fail on the next gate even after `src_id` fix |
| `role: ignored` | not in wrangler's allowed set | Same line range | Would hard-fail if any ignored source appears (Tejal corpus has none; dodged for attempt-2) |

**Forensic evidence preserved (gitignored; local-only):**
- `state/config/runs/6a3393f8-f369-4a30-b7c1-b50c60c1d1a2/directive.yaml` — §02A-composed directive (sha256 `351a57fbe12aff4a49349c4a646618d92ae38a798ec53eee61668f74f8bbd703`; size 4192 bytes; 11 sources). Reference baseline for next-session diff comparison.
- `state/config/runs/6a3393f8-f369-4a30-b7c1-b50c60c1d1a2/run.json` — trial envelope at point of crash; `status: in-flight`, `completed_at: null`, `production_clone_launch_evidence_reason: registered-no-specialist-fired`.
- Reproduced wrangler error message: `[run_wrangler] directive error: sources[0] missing required field: ref_id`

**Why this is Epic-scope, not a one-line patch:** Story 7c.3a authored the §02A composer as a fresh schema without verifying it conforms to **any** downstream consumer. The §02A composer's own test suite (5 files, 12 tests) verifies the composer-in-isolation but never feeds output into the wrangler. AM-11 launch-permission token (52/52 GREEN) tests preflight + readiness fixtures, not end-to-end specialist dispatch. The Murat M-A1 wiring-contract test added in SCP-2026-05-21-trial3-wiring tests the adapter-to-composer contract but mocks `compose()` itself — it cannot detect output-shape drift. **Every §02A→downstream boundary is unprobed.**

**Resolution scope (Epic-level):**

**Phase A — comprehensive probe (~30-45 min next session):** Before any fix lands, audit ALL §02A→downstream integration surfaces. Targets:
- Texas wrangler input schema (this surface; surface more drift in the rest of `run_wrangler.py` beyond `ref_id` + `role`)
- Texas bundle output → Irene Pass-1 input (does Irene read fields that the new wrangler bundle produces in a different shape?)
- Irene packet → §04 G1 decision card input
- §04A per-plan-unit row schema
- §04.55 run-constants lock structure
- §07C storyboard build input/output
- §11 voice-selection input
- §15 final bundle output shape

Each surface gets a `grep` + `Read` audit; the result is a full integration-drift inventory (zero finding → schema is clean; N findings → batch into Phase B fix).

**Phase B — batched fix (1-2 sessions, scope-dependent):**
- **Decision point ratified at party-mode:** harmonize §02A→canonical or harmonize-downstream-to-§02A? The §02A schema is the NEWER authored deliverable (Story 7c.3a); the wrangler + downstream consumers reflect the pre-§02A canonical. Honoring "newer schema is canonical" → update wrangler + consumers. Honoring "minimize-blast-radius" → revert §02A to match the existing canonical.
- Either direction: requires substrate amendment (TW-7c-4 allowlist extension + lockstep test updates) via formal SCP route. Likely larger Epic than the wiring SCP (multi-file, multi-specialist).
- Consider authoring as an **integration-coherence Epic** via `bmad-create-epics-and-stories` with stories per affected surface.

**Phase C — closure (Trial-3 attempt-3 re-launch):** Once Phase B lands, re-launch from `course-content/courses/tejal-apc-c1-m1-p2-trends/`. Same corpus; same trial protocol. The Phase A audit + Phase B fix should de-risk additional integration-drift surprises within the §02A→downstream chain.

**Reactivation trigger:** immediate (next session is the BMAD sprint specifically dedicated to this Epic, per operator directive 2026-05-21T22:30: *"Start next session with a BMAD sprint to correct and address as many related issues as can be identified now and corrected proactively."*).

**Cross-reference:**
- Sibling-class finding: `marcus-interactive-experience-not-delivered-by-slab-7c` (Epic-scope; post-Trial-3 successor). That Epic is downstream of Trial-3 closure; THIS Epic is the gate before Trial-3 can re-launch successfully.
- Parent SCP (closes the wiring blocker that surfaced this gap): `_bmad-output/planning-artifacts/sprint-change-proposal-2026-05-21-trial3-wiring.md`.
- Pattern: this is the SECOND "tested module, untested integration" gap in the same trial-launch arc — worth flagging as a Mary-tier anti-pattern candidate for cross-trial-learnings.

NOT Trial-3-blocking — Trial-3 ships against the CLI surface as-is. Reactivation trigger: **post-Trial-3 retrospective.** Likely Epic-scope, not single-story; needs `bmad-create-prd` → architecture → UX → stories chain.

| Entry | Filed | Trigger context | Resolution shape |
|---|---|---|---|
| **`marcus-interactive-experience-not-delivered-by-slab-7c`** | 2026-05-21 | **Architectural finding the operator surfaced post-Trial-3-cancellation review:** at trial launch the operator invokes `python -m app.marcus.cli trial start ...` directly; the operator-facing surface at G0 is a raw four-letter CLI prompt (`[c/e/s/x]`). Marcus-the-conversational-persona ([skills/bmad-agent-marcus/SKILL.md](skills/bmad-agent-marcus/SKILL.md)) is NOT in this runtime path. The SKILL.md promise — *"the operator should never need to think about agents, skills, APIs, or state; you are the interface; you carry the complexity"* — does not hold at the trial-launch surface. **Three distinct things named "Marcus" coexist and the naming collision masked the gap:** (1) Marcus-the-persona (BMAD skill at `skills/bmad-agent-marcus/`; sanctum at `_bmad/memory/bmad-agent-marcus/`; lives in Claude Code conversation space); (2) `app/marcus/` (Python package; LangGraph orchestrator runtime; trial CLI; gate runner; production runner); (3) `pre_gate_marcus` (LLM node inside `app/marcus/orchestrator/` that pre-fills gate proposals — a third meaning of the name). The Slab-7c work delivered (2) and (3) but did not bridge to (1). At the most operator-critical moments (G0, G1.5 IRREVERSIBLE lock, G3 IRREVERSIBLE four-artifact lock), the operator interacts with raw CLI verbs, not with Marcus-narrated context. **Implication:** the operator-mediation promise on which days of conversational-Marcus work were predicated has not been integration-delivered; the trial-launch surface is the CLI, with Marcus as a parallel doc/planning layer. | **Resolution scope:** Epic-level, not story-level. Likely shape: (a) `bmad-create-prd` for "Marcus-as-trial-launch-surface" Epic — operator says "Marcus, start a Trial-N run on corpus X" → Marcus reads the directive aloud → conversational G0 → Marcus invokes `app.marcus.cli` under the hood and narrates each gate transition with sanctum-loaded context; (b) Winston architecture pass on the bridge between Claude-Code-conversation-space (Marcus-skill) and Python-subprocess-space (`app/marcus/cli`) — IPC shape, state-sync, error-propagation; (c) Sally UX pass on the conversational gate surfaces (what does conversational G0 look like vs `[c/e/s/x]`? what does conversational G1.5 lock confirmation look like?); (d) story decomposition; (e) Trial-4 launches against the Marcus-mediated surface as success criterion. **Naming-collision sub-finding:** resolve the three-Marcuses ambiguity at architecture time. Candidate names: Marcus-Persona / Marcus-Runtime / Marcus-PreGate, or rename `app/marcus/` to something orthogonal. Architecture-level decision; not arbitrary. **Reactivation trigger:** post-Trial-3 retrospective consultation of this register per [CLAUDE.md §Deferred inventory governance](../../CLAUDE.md) binding-consultation-point #1. **Operator priority signal (2026-05-21):** "get to building out the promised but not delivered Marcus 'interactive' experience" — sequenced strictly AFTER CLI-only Trial-3 run completes. |

**Cross-reference:** complements the existing `slab-7c-marcus-cli-bypass` framing IF such an entry exists (none found at filing time — this is the first formal record of the gap). The Trial-3-blocking §02A composer wiring finding above is a RELATED but ORTHOGONAL gap: §02A wiring is the *specific* substrate-coherence defect that surfaced at G0; the Marcus-interactive gap is the *architectural* layer-mismatch finding that the §02A symptom revealed. ## POST-TRIAL-3 ARCHITECTURE — Workflow registry + Marcus-SPOC selection front-door (operator signal 2026-06-25)

**Status:** **POST-TRIAL-3 ARCHITECTURE FOLLOW-ON.** Surfaced 2026-06-25 when the operator, reviewing the Marcus duality, observed that the app will run MANY production types (narrated-slides-with-motion-video is one core example; a **podcast** run is another) and that the runtime needs to interact with the operator at the **front door to pick the workflow** before the run executes deterministically. NOT blocking — single-workflow (narrated-lesson) trials run against the existing `state/config/pipeline-manifest.yaml`. This entry **consolidates three previously-scattered threads** so the capability is not re-derived each time it surfaces. Reactivation trigger: **operator-priority decision on a new content type** (same trigger as Epic 18-7), OR **post-Trial-3 retrospective**.

| Entry | Filed | Trigger context | Resolution shape |
|---|---|---|---|
| **`marcus-spoc-workflow-selection-front-door`** | 2026-06-25 | **Operator architectural signal during the Marcus-duality discussion.** Each production type = its own pipeline-manifest (the manifest IS the workflow definition; `app/manifest/compiler.py` compiles manifest → LangGraph `StateGraph`). Today there is exactly ONE real workflow manifest (`state/config/pipeline-manifest.yaml`); `--preset production\|explore` is a quality/exploration knob and structural-walk `standard/motion/cluster.yaml` are variants of the SAME narrated-lesson family — NOT distinct types. Run/workflow SELECTION is an acknowledged stub: `scripts/marcus_capabilities/pr_rs.py` — *"PR-RS — Run Selection (stub): follow-up in story 26-10."* Operator model confirmed this session: **Marcus-SPOC** interacts at the FRONT DOOR to (a) pick the workflow from a registry + (b) seed initial guidance (theme, source content, research scope, lesson-plan contents) → the run then executes DETERMINISTICALLY → SPOC narrates each gate and threads operator choices to specialists as guidance. **Requires NO autonomous orchestrator:** selection is a bounded, operator-confirmed choice over a known registry; the existing deterministic-guard pattern (LLM advises/narrates, human decides, engine executes) extends to the front door. Determinism-after-selection preserves frozen-graph replay + tamper-evident HIL authority. | **Consolidates: Epic 18-7** (workflow-family framework — "18-7 gates all others; trigger = operator-priority decision on new content type") **+ Epic 18-5** (podcasts ship as a NEW pack family per [Pack Versioning Policy](../../docs/dev-guide/pipeline-manifest-regime.md#pack-versioning-policy), not v5 of narrated-lesson) **+ PR-RS / story-26-10** (the selection step itself) **+ the Marcus-SPOC surface** (where the picker lives). Likely shape: **(a)** a workflow **registry** (menu of manifests + metadata: id, display name, required inputs, specialist roster); **(b)** a front-door **selection turn** on the Marcus-SPOC surface (`app/marcus/cli/marcus_interlocutor.py` / `marcus_spoc.py`) — operator picks (optionally Marcus-advised), confirms; **(c)** **reproducibility** — freeze chosen workflow id + manifest content-hash + seed choices into the run envelope; **(d)** per-type manifests authored as new families (18-5 podcast first candidate). **Reactivation trigger:** operator picks a second content type (e.g., podcast) OR post-Trial-3 retrospective. **Direction may flip if substrate evolves** — if the Marcus-interactive Epic re-architects gate transport, re-validate the registry/selection attach-point at dispatch. |

**Cross-reference:** directly extends [`marcus-interactive-experience-not-delivered-by-slab-7c`](#post-trial-3-architecture--marcus-interactive-experience-not-delivered-by-slab-7c-filed-2026-05-21) (the Marcus-SPOC surface this front-door lives on). That entry's **naming-collision sub-finding is now partly resolved**: the runtime conversational surface was renamed **Marcus-SPOC** on 2026-06-25 (operator-facing callsign only — package `app.marcus`, function names, and the `"marcus"` model tier unchanged), making it distinct from BMAD-persona **Marcus** (`skills/bmad-agent-marcus/`, has the sanctum) and from the deterministic **`production_runner`** orchestration engine (not an agent). The braid-arc SPOC conversational layer already SHIPPED; this entry adds the workflow-SELECTION capability on top of it. Backlog authority: **Epic 18** (Backlog Epics table above) + near-term-candidate "Epic 18-7 workflow-family framework (if operator prioritizes new content types)."

**Status:** **POST-TRIAL-3 CONTENT-QUALITY FOLLOW-ON.** Surfaced 2026-06-11 when the operator asked for a substrate study of the slide-clustering + reading-path-pattern capabilities ahead of a planned enhancement (expand the Z-pattern success to triptych / image-dominant-first / other scan patterns). Explains the standing user complaint that narration does not follow the natural scan of slide content. NOT attempt-4-blocking. Reactivation trigger: **post-Trial-3 retrospective**, with the operator's per-slide scan-order nit harvest from the attempt-4 G2C/G3 storyboard reviews as the evidence corpus.

| Entry | Filed | Trigger context | Resolution shape |
|---|---|---|---|
| **`reading-path-enforcement-machinery-not-absorbed-at-severance`** 🔴 ESCALATED | 2026-06-11 (🔴 operator-escalated DISASTER-LEVEL 2026-06-19 PM) | **🔴 2026-06-19 PM: MERGE with `beta-narration-hallucinates-nonexistent-illustrations` into ONE #1-priority "perception + reading-path narrative-grounding restoration & ENHANCEMENT" arc.** Operator declared the combined loss (perception + reading-path/Z-pattern visual-structure that directed narrative focus) a disaster-level regression; mandate is REPAIR *and* ENHANCE next session. The reading-path classification is the structure half; the perception layer is the grounding half — both lost at severance, both needed for narration that speaks to what's on the slide in the order the eye reads it. — **Capability-degradation finding from read-only substrate study.** The primary repo's reading-path system was a 5-part lockstep: enum registry (`state/config/reading-path-patterns.yaml`), `reading_path` sub-object in `segment-manifest.schema.json`, pattern-aware emission lint (`scripts/validators/pass_2_emission_lint.py`; `sequence_numbered` FAIL-CLOSED, others warning), heuristic pattern classifier (`scripts/utilities/reading_path_classifier.py` `_SCORERS`), and the worked-examples doc — kept aligned by `tests/contracts/test_reading_path_parity.py`. Per `upstream-severance-log.md` (2026-04-24), ONLY the worked-examples doc was absorbed (`skills/bmad-agent-content-creator/references/pass-2-grammar-riders-examples.md`, loaded as in-context expertise by `app/specialists/irene/graph.py:67-68`); registry, schema enum, lint, classifier, and parity test were explicitly NOT absorbed. The hybrid Pass-2 contract (`app/specialists/irene/authoring/pass_2_template.py::SegmentManifestSegment`) has NO `reading_path` field — scan-order narration is enforced only by LLM adherence to in-context exemplars ("classify → declare → lint" degraded to "suggest"). Perception substrate survived (`PerceptionArtifact.visual_elements`, `VisualReference.location_on_slide`, `traceable_visual_references` rule) and is the better v2 foundation. v1 repertoire (7 patterns): z_pattern, f_pattern, center_out, top_down, multi_column, grid_quadrant, sequence_numbered — `multi_column` and `center_out` already approximate the operator's triptych / hero-image-first ambitions. | **Resolution scope:** compact "reading-path v2" Epic or story family; operator priority signal 2026-06-11 (planned enhancement; addresses standing user complaint). Phased shape: **(1) restore the contract natively** (do NOT re-absorb upstream code — severance re-open is a party-mode governance exception; rewrite under the schema-story scaffold): `reading_path` sub-object on `SegmentManifestSegment` (closed pattern enum + declared scan order + classifier confidence) + regenerated schema + pattern-conformance check in Irene's 9-node **verify** node (replaces the old standalone lint); **(2) perception-grounded extraction**: classify layout pattern from Gary's rendered PNGs between §07 and §08 (vision call w/ bounding-box evidence into `PerceptionArtifact`), so Pass 2 consumes a declared pattern rather than guessing; **(3) evidence-first repertoire growth**: add `triptych` (vs multi_column) / `image_dominant_first` (vs center_out) ONLY where Storyboard-B review evidence shows the 7 mis-fit real slides; each addition costs the full parity set (registry/schema/lint-check/classifier-scorer/worked example); new patterns enter at warning severity. Orthogonal to `marcus-interactive-experience-not-delivered-by-slab-7c` — can interleave. **Direction may flip if substrate evolves** — if a future pack version restructures Pass-2 authoring or the perception layer, re-validate the attach points (verify-node check; §07→§08 classification step) at dispatch rather than executing this shape blindly. |

| Item | What | Disposition |
|---|---|---|
| 🔴 **`motion-plan-producer-substrate-missing` (Tier-2)** | No migrated node emits per-slide motion designation: CD has no slides, marcus 07D/G2M is a dispatch no-op, gary rows lack a motion field, Irene Pass-1 has no `motion_brief` (April's came from the old skill-Irene). ## Production-envelope/bundle EXTRAORDINARY-ROBUSTNESS hardening arc (filed 2026-06-30; operator-emphatic architectural imperative)

- 🔴 **`bundle-carrier-extraordinary-robustness`** — owner: architecture (Winston) + Marcus orchestrator. The side-car that threads ALL workstream state — **`ProductionEnvelope`** (`app/models/runtime/production_envelope.py:100`, `contributions` + `add_contribution`) wrapped by `ProductionTrialEnvelope`, persisted as the bundle/run-dir (run.json/checkpoint.json/bundle_dir + g0-enrichment/segment-manifest/coverage-receipt/specialist outputs) — must be **EXTRAORDINARILY ROBUST** because every DEFERRED future consumer (enrichment, callbacks, lesson planning, multiple authored asset families) piles onto it; a weak carrier silently corrupts every downstream and the blast radius grows with each deferred feature. **Robustness contract (all required):** (1) schema-validated + `schema_version` + ADDITIVE-safe evolution (new field/asset-family never breaks an old reader); (2) append-only + `output_digest` provenance + first-wins idempotent re-dispatch (never silent-overwrite/drop); (3) FAIL-LOUD on missing/malformed/contradictory state (never silent-assume); (4) resumable + deterministic across pause/resume/recover with BOTH runner walks reading consistently ([[project-production-runner-two-walks]]); (5) single-SSOT — no shadow side-stores that drift (cf. the 5 scattered Gamma config stores, `gamma-styleguide-library-briefing-2026-06-30.md`); (6) new consumers read FROM the envelope in-graph (provenance > disk). **Shape (party-greenlit arc):** a carrier-coherence validator + schema-version/additive-evolution discipline + a fail-loud-on-corruption sweep + a contract test that a new contribution/asset-family round-trips through persist→resume→recover without loss. **Reactivate:** before the deferred consumers (callbacks beyond Leg-1b, lesson-plan materialization, new asset families) attach in volume — harden the carrier FIRST. Memory: [[feedback_bundle_carrier_extraordinarily_robust]]. Direction-stable (additive hardening; never relaxes a fail-loud gate).

Reported-not-fixed under the Leg-4 close guardrail (no rushed fix on a load-bearing dispatch path); owns its own RED-first cycle.
